#####ATHENA NEBULA#####

sys_tomaros_init = {
	name = "Tomaros"
	class = sc_g
	init_effect = {
		generate_home_system_resources = yes
	}

	max_instances = 1

	flags = { tomaros_system asari_republics_system canon_map }

	planet = {
		name = "Tomaros"
		class = pc_g_star
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = 1
		size = 16
		has_ring = no
		flags = { tomaros_star }
		init_effect = {
			add_deposit = d_energy_4
		}		
	}
	
	planet = {
		name = "Lusia"
		class = pc_tropical
        orbit_distance = 125
		orbit_angle = 110
		size = 21
		has_ring = no
		modifiers = none
		entity = "coastal_planet_06_entity"
		flags = { subclass_world }
		init_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					exists = event_target:asari_republics
				}
				create_colony = {
					owner = event_target:asari_republics
				}
				generate_btr_start_deposits_and_blockers = yes
				generate_asr_lusia_colony_buildings = yes	
				generate_asr_lusia_pops = yes
				clear_blockers = yes
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				log = "Asari Republics Colony - Lusia Spawned"
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = coastal_world
				days = -1
			}
		}
	}
	
	planet = {
		name = "Niagolon"
		class = pc_gas_giant
        orbit_distance = 125
		orbit_angle = -160
		size = 34
		has_ring = yes
		init_effect = {
			# add_deposit = d_helium_3_3
			add_deposit = d_exotic_gases_3
		}		
	}
	
	planet = {
		name = "Pronoia"
		class = pc_ice_giant
        orbit_distance = 125
		orbit_angle = 100
		size = 24
		has_ring = no
		init_effect = {
			# add_deposit = d_helium_3_3
			add_deposit = d_exotic_gases_3
			add_deposit = d_trade_value_4
		}			
	}
	
	planet = {
		name = "Beness"
		class = pc_ice_giant
        orbit_distance = 125
		orbit_angle = 100
		size = 26
		has_ring = no
		init_effect = {
			add_deposit = d_exotic_gases_2
		}	
	}	

	init_effect = { 
		spawn_megastructure = { 
			type = "athenanebula_sileannebula_primaryrelay" 
			name = "Athena 1 Relay"
			orbit_angle = 270 
			orbit_distance = 500
		} 
	}
}

	planet = {

        orbit_distance = 125

		size = 15

		init_effect = {
			add_deposit = d_engineering_3
		}	
	}
	
	planet = {
		name = "Niacal"
		class = pc_mephitic_station
        orbit_distance = 125
		orbit_angle = 90
		size = 25
		has_ring = no
		modifiers = none
		flags = { subclass_world }
		init_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					exists = event_target:asari_republics
				}
				set_planet_flag = planetary_station
				set_planet_flag = research_station				
				set_planet_flag = niacal_planet
				set_deposit_flags = yes
				create_colony = {
					owner = event_target:asari_republics
				}
				generate_btr_start_deposits_and_blockers = yes
				generate_asr_niacal_colony_buildings = yes	
				generate_asr_niacal_pops = yes
				clear_blockers = yes
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				add_deposit = d_mephitic_blocker
				add_deposit = d_arborary_oasis
				log = "Asari Republics Colony - Niacal Spawned"
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = lush_planet
				days = -1
			}
		}
	}

sys_loropi_init = {
    name = "Loropi"
    class = sc_a
	init_effect = {
		generate_home_system_resources = yes
		save_global_event_target_as = asariThirdFleet
	}

	max_instances = 1

	flags = { loropi_system asari_republics_system canon_map }

	asteroid_belt = {
		type = icy_asteroid_belt
		radius = 490
	}

    planet = {
	    name = "Loropi"
        class = pc_a_star
        orbit_distance = 0
        size = 27
		flags = { loropi_star }
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Paphos"
        class = pc_gas_giant
        orbit_distance = 250
        orbit_angle = 21
        size = 37
        has_ring = yes
		init_effect = {
			# add_deposit = d_helium_3_2
			add_deposit = d_exotic_gases_2
		}
    }

	planet = {
        name = "Espota Station"
        class = pc_habitat
        orbit_distance = 125
        orbit_angle = 117
        size = 3
        has_ring = no
		modifiers = none
		flags = { espota_station }
		init_effect = {
			add_deposit = d_energy_8
			add_deposit = d_exotic_gases_4
			if = {
				limit = { 
					exists = event_target:asari_republics
				}
				create_colony = {
					owner = event_target:asari_republics
				}
				generate_asr_espota_station_buildings = yes	
				generate_asr_espota_pops = yes
				clear_blockers = yes
				prevent_anomaly = yes
				log = "Asari Republics Colony - Espota Station Spawned"
			}
		}
	}

    planet = {
        name = "Yasilium"
        class = pc_iron
        orbit_distance = 125
        orbit_angle = 117
        size = 6
        has_ring = no
	}	

	init_effect = { 
		spawn_megastructure = { 
			type = "sileannebula_prodicatoresscar_primaryrelay" 
			name = "Silean 2 Relay"
			orbit_angle = 270 
			orbit_distance = 500
		} 
	}
}

sys_strabo_init = {
    name = "Strabo"
    class = sc_g
	init_effect = {
		generate_home_system_resources = yes
	}

	max_instances = 1

    flags = { strabo_system salarian_union_system canon_map }

	asteroid_belt = {
		type = rocky_asteroid_belt
		radius = 50
	}	

    planet = {
		name = "Strabo"
        class = pc_g_star
        orbit_distance = 0
        size = 30
		flags = { strabo_star }
		init_effect = {
			add_deposit = d_energy_4
			create_ambient_object = {
				type = "nebula_2"
				entity_offset_height = -5
				location = this
			}
			last_created_ambient_object = {
				set_location = {
					target = prev
					distance = 0
					angle = random
				}
			}
		}
    }

    planet = {
        name = "Antigar"
        class = pc_gas_giant
        orbit_distance = 250
        orbit_angle = 174
        has_ring = yes
		size = 27
		init_effect = {
			# add_deposit = d_helium_3_2
